   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of ongoing armed conflicts
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>

     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="hatnote">
      For recent conflicts that are no longer significantly ongoing, see
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_wars_2011%E2%80%93present" title="List of wars 2011present">
       List of wars 2011present
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_number_of_conflicts_per_year" title="List of number of conflicts per year">
       List of number of conflicts per year
      </a>
      .
     </div>

      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:452px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="289" data-file-width="512" height="254" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg/450px-Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg/675px-Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg/900px-Ongoing_conflicts_around_the_world.svg.png 2x" width="450"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">

        <center>
         Locations of ongoing conflicts worldwide, June 2015
        </center>
        <div class="legend">
         <span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:maroon; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">
         </span>
         Major wars, 10,000+ deaths in current or past year
        </div>
        <div class="legend">
         <span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:red; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">
         </span>
         Wars, 1,0009,999 deaths in current or past year
        </div>
        <div class="legend">
         <span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:orange; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">
         </span>
         Minor conflicts, 100-999 deaths in current or past year
        </div>
        <div class="legend">
         <span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:gold; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">
         </span>
         Skirmishes and clashes, fewer than 100 deaths in current or past year
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      The following is a
      <b>
       list of ongoing
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Armed_conflicts" title="Armed conflicts">
        armed conflicts
       </a>
      </b>
      that are taking place around the world and continue to result in violence.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <p>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="List_guidelines">
       List guidelines
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List guidelines">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      This list of ongoing armed conflicts is for the sole purpose of identifying present-day conflicts and the death toll associated with each conflict. The guidelines of inclusion are:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Armed conflicts consist in the use of armed force between two or more organized armed groups, governmental or non-governmental alike.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         1
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Interstate, intrastate and non-state armed conflicts are listed. For ongoing civil unrest and violence against protesters not escalating into armed conflict, see
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_ongoing_protests" title="List of ongoing protests">
        List of ongoing protests
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Fatality figures include battle-related deaths (military and civilian) as well as civilians intentionally targeted by the parties to an armed conflict. Only direct deaths resulting from violence are included for the current and past year; excess deaths indirectly resulting from famine, disease and disruption of services are included along with violent deaths only in the cumulative fatalities count, when available.
      </li>
      <li>
       Listed conflicts are at least 100 cumulative deaths in total and at least 1 death in current or past calendar year.
      </li>
      <li>
       Fatality totals may be underestimated or unavailable due to a lack of information. A figure with a plus sign indicates that at least that many people have died (e.g. 455+ indicates that at least 455 people have died) - the actual toll could be considerably higher.
      </li>
      <li>
       Location refers to the state(s) where the main violence takes place, not to the warring parties. Italics indicate disputed territories and
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">
        unrecognized states
       </a>
       <i>
        .
       </i>
      </li>
      <li>
       Only states with ongoing military activity are listed, past states and states where conflicts are no longer active are omitted.
      </li>
      <li>
       Military conflicts that no longer produce violence are not listed here, but can be found in the historical
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_wars" title="List of wars">
        list of wars
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_wars_extended_by_diplomatic_irregularity" title="List of wars extended by diplomatic irregularity">
        list of wars extended by diplomatic irregularity
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      <span id="Major_wars">
      </span>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="10.2C000_or_more_deaths_in_current_or_past_year">
       10,000 or more deaths in current or past year
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 10,000 or more deaths in current or past year">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Conflicts in the following list have caused at least 10,000 direct violent deaths in current or past calendar year.

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1.2C000.E2.80.939.2C999_deaths_in_current_or_past_year">
       1,0009,999 deaths in current or past year
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1,0009,999 deaths in current or past year">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Conflicts in the following list have caused at least 1,000 and fewer than 10,000 direct violent deaths in current or past calendar year.
      <br/>
      Conflicts causing at least 1,000 deaths in one calendar year are considered wars by the
      <a href="/wiki/Uppsala_Conflict_Data_Program" title="Uppsala Conflict Data Program">
       Uppsala Conflict Data Program
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated8_42-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated8-42">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        35
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <table class="wikitable sortable">
      <tr>
       <th>
        Start of conflict

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="100.E2.80.93999_deaths_in_current_or_past_year">
       100999 deaths in current or past year
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 100999 deaths in current or past year">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Conflicts in the following list have caused at least 100 and fewer than 1,000 direct violent deaths in current or past calendar year.
     </p>
     <table class="wikitable sortable">

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Fewer_than_100_deaths_in_current_or_past_year">
       Fewer than 100 deaths in current or past year
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Fewer than 100 deaths in current or past year">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Conflicts in the following list have caused at least 1 and fewer than 100 direct violent deaths in current or past calendar year.
     </p>
     <table class="wikitable sortable">
      <tr>
       <th>
        Start of conflict

        Location
       </th>
       <th data-sort-type="number">
        Cumulative fatalities
       </th>
       <th data-sort-type="number">
        Fatalities in 2014
       </th>
       <th data-sort-type="number">
        Fatalities in 2015
       </th>
      </tr>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Deaths_by_country">
       Deaths by country
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Deaths by country">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      This section details armed conflict-related fatalities by country in 2013 and 2014 based on the Project for the Study of the 21st Century.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AAA_44-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-AAA-44">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        37
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <br/>
      Mexico, Egypt and Kenya are not included into this project but should appear and therefore have been added.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-441">
       <a href="#cite_note-441">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        398
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-442">
       <a href="#cite_note-442">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        399
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="483" data-file-width="635" height="266" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png/350px-2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png/525px-2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/6b/2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png 2x" width="350"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2013-2014_fatalities_in_world_conflicts.png" title="Enlarge">

        </div>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">
       External links
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_ongoing_armed_conflicts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: External links">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.systemicpeace.org/warlist/warlist.htm" rel="nofollow">
        Major Episodes of Political Violence 1946-2014
       </a>
       - List of armed conflicts compiled by Dr. Monty G. Marshall, director of the Center for Systemic Peace, based on research sponsored by the
       <a href="/wiki/Political_Instability_Task_Force" title="Political Instability Task Force">
        Political Instability Task Force
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.ucdp.uu.se/gpdatabase/search.php" rel="nofollow">
        UCDP Conflict Encyclopedia
       </a>
       -
       <a href="/wiki/Uppsala_Conflict_Data_Program" title="Uppsala Conflict Data Program">
        Uppsala Conflict Data Program
       </a>
       of the Department of Peace and Conflict Research at
       <a href="/wiki/Uppsala_University" title="Uppsala University">
        Uppsala University
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.crisisgroup.org/en/publication-type/crisiswatch.aspx" rel="nofollow">
        CrisisWatch
       </a>
       - Monthly bulletin, interactive map and database on ongoing conflicts by the
       <a href="/wiki/International_Crisis_Group" title="International Crisis Group">
        International Crisis Group
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.peri.umass.edu/index.php?id=396" rel="nofollow">
        Modern Conflicts Database
       </a>
        2007 Database of all post-Cold War conflicts with estimated death tolls of 25,000 or more, by the Political Economy Research Institute of the
       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Massachusetts_Amherst" title="University of Massachusetts Amherst">
        University of Massachusetts Amherst
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.globalsecurity.org/military/world/war/" rel="nofollow">
        Global Security coverage of ongoing wars
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.warsintheworld.com/" rel="nofollow">
        Wars in the world
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.historyguy.com/21st_century_wars.html" rel="nofollow">
        History Guy's coverage of 21st century wars
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.HIIK.de/" rel="nofollow">
        Heidelberg Institute for International Conflict Research (HIIK)
       </a>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <a class="external text" href="http://www.hiik.de/en/konfliktbarometer/index.html" rel="nofollow">
          Conflict Barometer
         </a>
         - Describes recent trends in conflict development, escalations, and settlements
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.insightonconflict.org/" rel="nofollow">
        Insight on Conflict
       </a>
       - Database on peace-building initiatives in areas of conflict
      </li>
     </ul>
